# Original graph

```mermaid
graph TD;
	0(" ");
	1(" ");
	2(" ");
	3(" ");
	4(" ");
	5(" ");
	6(" ");
	7(" ");
	0 --- 1;
	0 --- 3;
	0 --- 5;
	0 --- 7;
	2 --- 1;
	2 --- 3;
	2 --- 5;
	2 --- 7;
	4 --- 1;
	4 --- 3;
	4 --- 5;
	4 --- 7;
	6 --- 1;
	6 --- 3;
	6 --- 5;
	6 --- 7;
```
